        <div class="dn-page-column-content">
          <div class="dn-widgets">  <div  class="dn-widget dn-widget-5f8914b7-0c7e-47f5-9c20-db7a335989d4 dn-widget-heading ah-heading-title gradient-text-green-blue dn-widget-margin-top-none dn-widget-margin-bottom-custom dn-mobile-align-left" style="z-index: 5;">
    <div class="dn-widget-content-container"><div class="dn-widget-content">
      <div contenteditable="false" id="5f8914b7-0c7e-47f5-9c20-db7a335989d4_heading" class="dn-heading" >
  <h3><meta charset="utf-8"><meta charset="utf-8">Our services are all about flawless customer experiences.</h3>

</div>

    </div></div>
  </div>
  <div  class="dn-widget dn-widget-2292604e-1508-49ea-a746-74eddbcd4bf0 dn-widget-heading h1 text-white dn-widget-margin-top-none dn-widget-margin-bottom-custom dn-mobile-align-left" style="z-index: 4;">
    <div class="dn-widget-content-container"><div class="dn-widget-content">
      <div contenteditable="false" id="2292604e-1508-49ea-a746-74eddbcd4bf0_heading" class="dn-heading" >
  <h2><meta charset="utf-8"><meta charset="utf-8">Why choose Garment Printing?</h2>

</div>

    </div></div>
  </div>
  <div  class="dn-widget dn-section-widget" style="z-index: 3;">
    <div class="dn-widget-content-container"><div class="dn-widget-content">
      <div  class="dn-page-section dn-page-section-e80ebd8c-6ac8-417a-be74-f568e88a6bc6  dn-mobile-align-center dn-page-section-cols-1 dn-page-section-spacing-default dn-page-section-margin-top-default dn-page-section-margin-bottom-none" id="dn_section_e80ebd8c-6ac8-417a-be74-f568e88a6bc6" style="z-index: 7;"><div><div class="dn-page-section-content"><div class="dn-padding-container" id="dn_s_pc_e80ebd8c-6ac8-417a-be74-f568e88a6bc6"><!--
  --><div class="dn-page-columns-container"><!--
    --><div  class="dn-page-column dn-page-column-variable dn-mobile-span12 dn-small-span12 dn-medium-span12 dn-large-span12 dn-page-column-first dn-page-column-last" id="dn_col_395b8453-2ed3-4c96-9ff8-69bfd7f01b15">
        
        <div class="dn-page-column-content">
          <div class="dn-widgets">  <div  class="dn-widget dn-widget-e9b36247-13ec-424a-8f30-dd18a9cc9d83 dn-widget-html_cm dn-widget-margin-top-none dn-widget-margin-bottom-none dn-mobile-align-left" style="z-index: 2;">
    <div class="dn-widget-content-container"><div class="dn-widget-content">
      <div class="gp-choose-card-holder">
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737478/f/f/t/0/1/opera-house--landmarks-NATIONAL-SYMBOL-ARCHITECTURE-BUILDING-AUSTRALIA-sydney-opera-house.svg?1601673900" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">100% Australian Based</h5>
      <p>100% Australian based commercial apparel printing company based in Sydney. We are committed to our local businesses and firmly adhere to the high standards that you can expect from a true Aussie business.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737488/f/f/t/0/1/oscard-award--rewards-trophy-oscar-STAR-ACADEMY-AWARDS-FILM-GOLD-WINNER.svg?1601674237" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Printed for Care</h5>
      <p>We have years of expertise working with corporate clients and have adapted our approach to best suit their needs. We use state-of-the-art printing machines, only the highest quality techniques and each order is accurately monitored so you get the apparel and merchandise your business deserves.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737513/f/f/t/0/1/tshirt%20printing%20studio.svg?1601675228" alt="logo-missing" />
     </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Amazing Design Studio</h5>
      <p>Customise any of our products by uploading your own artworks, logo, pictures, or text. We have also over 10,000 designs to choose from. Our design studio is easy to use by both experienced graphic designers and those starting out.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737523/f/f/t/0/1/no%20hiiden%20costs.svg?1601676253" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">No Hidden Costs</h5>
      <p>We hate hidden charges and we know, you
too! We don't charge any extra setup fee or
artwork charges - everything is discussed in
detail before we start working on your project!</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737608/f/f/t/0/1/eco%20friendly%20printing.svg?1601678098" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Socially Responsible</h5>
      <p>At Garment Printing, we recognise the impact of all our actions. Most of our apparel is ethically sourced, and we use eco-friendly inks which are Oeko-Tex Standard 100 certified.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737603/f/f/t/0/1/bulk%20order%20discounts.svg?1601678098" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Bulk Order Discounts</h5>
      <p>We can handle any order, no matter how big it may be. Moreover, we have enticing bulk order discounts to drive the price per unit down as you order more. Get in touch with us, so we can provide you with a customised quote.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  
  
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737598/f/f/t/0/1/no%20minimum%20order.svg?1601678098" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">No Minimums</h5>
      <p>We also accept short runs and have not placed any minimum quantity restrictions for Direct to Garment printing and Vinyl Transfer printing. So order now with ease.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737623/f/f/t/0/1/All%20kind%20of%20printing.svg?1601678785" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Printing Solutions</h5>
      <p>We offer a range of printing methods for you to choose from such as Direct to Garment, Vinyl Transfers, Screen Printing, Embroidery, Digital Full Colour Transfer, Sublimation, and much more. If you do not know which printing technique will work best, worry no more!</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737618/f/f/t/0/1/print%20on%20demand%20dropshipping.svg?1601678784" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Value for Money</h5>
      <p>Price is a major consideration for all purchases any business makes. We are committed to providing you with the best affordable prices and that too with no sacrifices in quality.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737628/f/f/t/0/1/free%20design%20review.svg?1601678785" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Fast Turnarounds</h5>
      <p>Our fast turnaround ensures we can meet any tight deadlines. You can avail our express delivery options if you are in a hurry. Have your custom printed apparel ready just when you need them.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737633/f/f/t/0/1/price%20beat%20guarantee.svg?1601679009" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Price Beat Guarantee</h5>
      <p>We are confident that we offer one of the most affordable pricing for custom uniform printing in Australia. This confidence is reflected in our price beat promise, where we guarantee to beat any lower quote you may find for a similar printing technique and service.</p>
    </article>
  </div>
  <div class="col">
    <article class="card-design gp-choose-card">
      <div class="img-holder">
        <img src="https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com/rshared/ssc/i/riq/4737638/f/f/t/0/1/proven%20track%20record.svg?1601679009" alt="logo-missing" />
      </div>
      <h5 class="h3">Easy Ordering</h5>
      <p>We know you have better things to do. So in our efforts not to distract you from growing your business, we have designed a simple and quick ordering process. You can choose to order via our website or just email us your specifications, and we will take it from there.</p>
    </article>
  </div>

      // Listen for messages from the iframe
      window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
        // Check the origin to ensure it's from the correct source
        if (event.origin === 'https://dnpreview_garmentprinting.secure-decoration.com') {
          // Access the contentDocument of the iframe
          var iframeDocument = iframe.contentDocument || iframe.contentWindow.document;
          // Apply styles to elements inside the iframe
          var labelElements = iframeDocument.getElementsByTagName('label');
          for (var i = 0; i < labelElements.length; i++) {
            labelElements[i].style.color = 'blue';
          }
        }
      });

    <script>
      // add dynamic colonical links according to url
      function addCanonicalLink() {
        let existingCanonicalLink = document.querySelector('link[rel="canonical"]');
        if (existingCanonicalLink) {
          // If a link exists, update its href
          existingCanonicalLink.href = determineCanonicalUrl();
        }else{
          let canonicalUrl = determineCanonicalUrl();
          // Create the link element
          let link = document.createElement('link');
          link.rel = 'canonical';
          link.href = canonicalUrl;
          document.head.appendChild(link);
        }
      }
      function determineCanonicalUrl() {
        if (window.location.href === 'https://garmentprinting.com.au/create?category=4137323') {
          return 'https://example.com/polos-men';
        } else {
          return window.location.href;
        }
      }
      addCanonicalLink();
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  if(typeof dnBehaviours !== 'undefined') {
    //runFuncOnLoad(function() {
      dnBehaviours.bind(null, true);
    //});
  }
  function appendCustomStyleSheets(nodeEl) {
    var sheets = document.styleSheets;
    for(var i=0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
      var sheet = sheets[i];
      if(sheet.href != null && sheet.href.trim() != "" && !sheet.href.includes("bundlev3")) {
        nodeEl.append('<link rel="stylesheet" href="' + sheet.href + '" type="text/css" media="all">\n');
      }
    }
  }
  function initPage() {
    if(typeof dnBehaviours !== 'undefined') {
      dnBehaviours.bind(null, false);
    } else {
      $dnj(document.body).addClass("dn-behaviours-bound");
    }
    $dnj.ajaxSetup({
      headers: { 'X-CSRF-Token': dnCSRFToken }
    });
    var addStylesNode = document.getElementById("deferred-styles");
    appendCustomStyleSheets(addStylesNode);
    var replacement = document.createElement("div");
    replacement.innerHTML = addStylesNode.textContent;
    document.body.appendChild(replacement)
    addStylesNode.parentElement.removeChild(addStylesNode);
    
    // 
    
    dnInitLazyLoad();
  }
</script>
